is O
that O

not O
block O
. O

of O

to O

for O

to O
finish O
before O
the O
action O
returns O

Answer_to_Question_ID O
: O

Question_URL O
: O

The O
thing O
is O
that O
Arduino B-Device
does O
n't O
use O
Processing B-Programming_Language
. O

Processing B-Programming_Language
is O
( O
was O
? O
) O
a O
separate O
programming O
language O
which O
was O
developed O
independently O
for O
a O
different O
purpose O
. O

The O
language O
resembles O
C B-Programming_Language
and O
C++ B-Programming_Language
very O
closely O
, O
so O
closely O
that O
it O
's O
almost O
identical O
. O

Programming O
the O
Arduino B-Device
, O
however O
, O
is O
accomplished O
using O
a O
( O
n O
unfortunate O
) O
mixture O
of O
C B-Programming_Language
and O
C++ B-Programming_Language
, O
with O
a O
set O
of O
custom O
libraries O
( O
which O
are O
similar O
in O
style O
to O
that O
of O
Processing B-Programming_Language
) O
. O

These O
libraries O
are O
written O
in O
C B-Programming_Language
and O
C++ B-Programming_Language
themselves O
, O
and O
they O
are O
only O
good O
for O
making O
one O
's O
code O
more O
portable O
across O
different O
MCU B-Device
types O
. O

Using O
them O
is O
not O
strictly O
necessary O
for O
programming O
the O
AVR B-Device
MCU I-Device
. O

In O
fact O
, O
the O
libraries O
have O
quite O
a O
few O
drawbacks O
( O
the O
code O
is O
big O
, O
inherently O
slow O
and O
ugly O
, O
amongst O
others O
) O
. O

If O
you O
want O
to O
use O
plain O
ol O
' O
C B-Programming_Language
for O
programming O
the O
Arduino B-Device
, O
then O
just O
go O
ahead O
and O
do O
so O
. O

Grab O
the O
reference O
PDF O
from O
Atmel B-Website
's O
site O
for O
your O
particular O
MCU B-Device
, O
learn O
the O
special O
registers B-Device
( O
I/O O
, O
timers O
, O
etc O
. O
) O
, O
install O
the O
avr-gcc B-Application
toolchain I-Application
on O
your O
computer O
, O
and O
use O
avr-gcc O
, O
avr-objcopy O
and O
avrdude O
to O
compile O
and O
install O
your O
programs O
. O

There O
also O
happens O
to O
be O
a O
C-only B-Programming_Language
library O
which O
follows O
this O
kind O
of O
convention O
. O

It O
does O
n't O
provide O
as O
much O
abstraction O
as O
the O
stock O
Arduino B-Programming_Language
library O
has O
, O
because O
it O
's O
lower-level O
, O
but O
you O
can O
have O
a O
look O
at O
it O
and O
see O
how O
one O
can O
accomplish O
basic O
algorithms O
without O
the O
default O
libraries O
. O

Essentially O
TransactionScope B-Library_Class
does O
n't O
track O
your O
Adapter O
's O
, O
what O
it O
does O
is O
it O
tracks O
database O
connections O
. O

When O
you O
open O
a O
DB O
connection O
the O
connections O
will O
looks O
if O
there O
is O
an O
ambient O
transaction O
( O
Transaction B-Library_Class
Scope I-Library_Class
) O
and O
if O
so O
enlist O
with O
it O
. O

Caution O
if O
there O
are O
more O
the O
one O
connection O
to O
the O
same O
SQL B-Application
server I-Application
this O
will O
escalate O
to O
a O
Distribtued O
Transaction O
. O

What O
happens O
since O
you O
're O
using O
a O
using O
block O
you O
are O
ensuring O
dispose O
will O
be O
called O
even O
if O
an O
exception B-Library_Class
occurs O
. O

So O
if O
dispose O
is O
called O
before O
txScope.Complete() O
the O
TransactionScope B-Library_Class
will O
tell O
the O
connections O
to O
rollback O
their O
transactions O
( O
or O
the O
DTC O
) O
. O

The O
TransactionScope B-Library_Class
class O
works O
with O
the O
Transaction B-Library_Class
class O
, O
which O
is O
thread-specific O
. O

When O
the O
TransactionScope B-Library_Class
is O
created O
, O
it O
checks O
to O
see O
if O
there O
is O
a O
Transaction B-Library_Class
for O
the O
thread O
; O
if O
one O
exists O
then O
it O
uses O
that O
, O
otherwise O
, O
it O
creates O
a O
new O
one O
and O
pushes O
it O
onto O
the O
stack B-Data_Structure
. O

If O
it O
uses O
an O
existing O
one O
, O
then O
it O
just O
increments O
a O
counter O
for O
releases O
( O
since O
you O
have O
to O
call O
Dispose O
on O
it O
) O
. O

On O
the O
last O
release O
, O
if O
the O
Transaction B-Library_Class
was O
not O
comitted O
, O
it O
rolls O
back O
all O
the O
work O
. O

As O
for O
why O
classes O
seem O
to O
magically O
know O
about O
transactions O
, O
that O
is O
left O
as O
an O
implementation O
detail O
for O
those O
classes O
that O
wish O
to O
work O
with O
this O
model O
. O

When O
you O
create O
your O
deptAdapter O
and O
emptAdapter O
instances O
, O
they O
check O
to O
see O
if O
there O
is O
a O
current O
transaction O
on O
the O
thread O
( O
the O
static O
Current B-Library_Class
property O
on O
the O
Transaction B-Library_Class
class O
) O
. O

If O
there O
is O
, O
then O
it O
registers O
itself O
with O
the O
Transaction B-Library_Class
, O
to O
take O
part O
in O
the O
commit/rollback O
sequence O
( O
which O
Transaction B-Library_Class
controls O
, O
and O
might O
propogate O
to O
varying O
transaction O
coordinators O
, O
such O
as O
kernel B-Application
, O
distributed O
, O
etc O
. O
) O
. O

OP_BLOCK O
: O
( O
output O
omitted O
for O
annotation O
) O

With O
4 O
threads O
per O
block O
you O
are O
only O
launching O
one O
warp O
per O
block O
. O

A O
warp O
is O
the O
unit O
of O
execution O
( O
and O
scheduling O
, O
and O
resource O
assignment O
) O
in O
CUDA B-Application
, O
not O
a O
thread O
. O

Currently O
, O
a O
warp O
consists O
of O
32 O
threads O
. O

This O
means O
that O
all O
4 O
of O
your O
threads O
per O
block O
( O
since O
there O
is O
no O
conditional O
behavior O
in O
this O
case O
) O
are O
executing O
in O
lockstep O
. O

When O
they O
reach O
the O
printf O
function O
call O
, O
they O
all O
execute O
the O
call O
to O
that O
function O
in O
the O
same O
line O
of O
code O
, O
in O
lockstep O
. O

So O
the O
question O
becomes O
, O
in O
this O
situation O
, O
how O
does O
the O
CUDA B-Application
runtime O
dispatch O
these O
" O
simultaneous O
" O
function O
calls O
? O

The O
answer O
to O
that O
question O
is O
unspecified O
, O
but O
it O
is O
not O
" O
random O
" O
. O

Therefore O
it O
's O
reasonable O
that O
the O
order O
of O
dispatch O
for O
operations O
within O
a O
warp O
does O
not O
change O
from O
run O
to O
run O
. O

If O
you O
launch O
enough O
threads O
to O
create O
multiple O
warps O
per O
block O
, O
and O
probably O
also O
include O
some O
other O
code O
to O
disperse O
and O
or O
" O
randomize O
" O
the O
behavior O
between O
warps O
, O
you O
should O
be O
able O
to O
see O
printf O
operations O
emanating O
from O
separate O
warps O
occurring O
in O
" O
random O
" O
order O
. O

Answer_to_Question_ID O
: O
30443827 O

Question_URL O
: O
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/30443827/ O

answer O
the O
second O
part O
of O
your O
question O
, O
when O
control O
flow O
diverges O
at O
the O
if O
statement O
, O
the O
threads O
where O
threadIdx.x O
!= O
0 O
simply O
wait O
to O
at O
the O
convergence O
point O
after O
the O
if O
statement O
. O

They O

not O
go O
on O
to O
the O
printf O
statement O
until O
thread O
0 O
has O
completed O
the O
if O
block O
. O

CODE_BLOCK O

Q_6040 O
( O

for O

Answer_to_Question_ID O
: O
46042992 O

Question_URL O
: O
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/46042992/ O


An O
explanation O
would O
be O
: O

Prototypes O
are O
live O
chains O
between O
objects O
. O

Because O
B O
's O
prototype O
is O
a O
single O
tone O
instance O
of O
A O
, O
the O
array B-Data_Structure
prop O
is O
passed O
by O
reference O
. O

This O
means O
that O
for O
each O
B O
instance O
we O
have O
access O
to O
the O
same O
A O
instance O
on O
the O
prototype O
. O

This O
might O
sound O
confusing O
at O
first O
but O
that O
's O
the O
magic O
of O
prototypes O
in O
JavaScript B-Programming_Language
. O

This O
is O
the O
caveat O
of O
prototypal O
inheritance O
. O

Anything O
on O
the O
prototype O
will O
be O
passed O
down O
to O
each O
instance O
. O

To O
maintain O
different O
instances O
of O
the O
attribute O
we O
initialise O
our O
object O
's O
attributes O
in O
the O
constructor O
. O

When O
working O
with O
objects O
in O

As O

pointed O
out O

. O

First O

're O

" O

" O

; O

. O

To O

while O

CODE_BLOCK O
: O

( O

omitted O
for O

) O

A_6463 O
( O

) O

In O
most O
situations O
, O
you O
cannot O
read O
cross O
domain O
cookies O
, O
for O
security O
reasons O
. O

Each O
cookie O
has O
a O
domain O
of O
definition O
, O
and O
your O
browser B-Application
reads O
those O
to O
decide O
which O
cookies O
you O
can O
read O
according O
to O
which O
domain O
you O
're O
on O
. O

If O
you O
have O
control O
of O
both O
domains O
, O
you O
can O
modify O
cookie O
settings O
on O
domain O
B O
to O
allow O
them O
to O
be O
read O
by O
domain O
A O
, O
or O
code O

cookie O
getter O
to O
get O
the O
values O
. O

Be O
creative O
! O
